韩服冒险岛公告


7/16(수) 몬스터파크 익스트림 자동 매칭 기능 임시 제한 안내





你好. 这里是冒险岛.


몬스터파크 익스트림 자동 매칭 관련된 문제가 확인되어

7월 16일(수) 오후 7시 13분 몬스터파크 익스트림 자동 매칭 기능 이용을 임시 제한했습니다.

오류 수정 이전까지 해당 기능 사용이 임시 제한될 예정이며,

수정이 완료되면 본 공지를 통해 다시 안내드리겠습니다.


게임 이용에 불편을 드려 죄송합니다.

더욱 안정적인 서비스를 제공하기 위해 노력하겠습니다.

[Completed] Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 16th July 2025


15 Jul 2025

[Completed] Server Check and Cash Shop Update on 16th July 2025


[Update as of 16th July 2025, 1154hrs]

Game services have resumed as of 1154hrs.

Thank you.


Dear Maplers,

Please be informed that there will be a scheduled maintenance on 16th July 2025.
During this period, services undergoing maintenance will be temporarily unavailable.

Game Maintenance
  • Maintenance Period: 16th July 2025, 0900hrs ~ 1200hrs
  • Affected Service(s): MapleStorySEA game servers
  • Impact: All MapleStorySEA game servers will be unavailable
    •   ↪ Game services for all worlds will not be available during the stipulated time. Kindly log out before this period to avoid disruptions to your gameplay.

    Website Maintenance
  • Maintenance Period: 16th July 2025, 1000hrs ~ 1200hrs
  • Affected Service(s): MapleStorySEA Passport Website
  • Impact: MapleStorySEA Passport services will be unavailable

    Update Preview
  • Cash Shop Update details for 16th July 2025 can be found here.


    • Thank you.

    - MapleSEA Administrator

    Abyssal Expedition: El Nath Mountains


    9th July 2025, (After Maintenance) ~ 19th August 2025, 2359hrs

    Developer Notes

    The Abyssal Expedition team has made its return to El Nath. Begin your expedition by enlisting mercenaries to battle through waves of monsters and gain experience as they progress.
    As your mercenaries grow stronger, you’ll face increasingly powerful bosses. Overcome these challenges to claim the final reward—The Abyssal Expedition Union Block.



    Available to Level 200+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest



    To start of your expedition, click the Maple Expedition button to bring up the UI.
    Double click on any of the mercenaries to add them to your team.



    Achieve the playtime daily and receive Expedition Supplies.
    As you increase your Command Rank, you will unlock more slots for mercenaries and better Expedition Supplies



    Once your mercenaries are set, use the portal at the left side of the map to start your journey!



    Depending on the level of the map, you can either enter the left white portal for grinding exp or the orange portal in the map for boss.
    As your mercenaries get stronger, you unlock maps with stronger monsters and bosses.



    Let the mercenaries do the job for you as they will attack the monsters automatically.
    Obtain EXP when monsters has been defeated.
    You can only stay on the map for a set duration.
    As you get stronger, you unlock more maps and stay on the map longer up to 8 hours daily.

    > Additional Information <

    Commander Skills
    To Position! (Cooldown 60 Seconds)
     ↪ Instantly moves all expedition members to the designated location without overlapping them.
    Rally (Cooldown 30 Seconds)
     ↪ Instantly moves all expedition members to your location, and generates a barrier for a set duration.
     ↪ Expedition members who enter the barrier temporarily receive protective effects and can evade Boss monsters' AoE attacks.
    Aim (Cooldown 30 Seconds)
     ↪ All expedition members focus their attacks on the monster designated by your character.
    Shout (Cooldown 4 Hours) [Unlocks at Veteran Rank and above]
     ↪ Lets out a powerful shout that boots the morale of all expedition members.
     ↪ All expedition members' ATT +50
     ↪ MSPD +20
     ↪ Attack Speed +2 levels
     ↪ Duration: 1 Hour

    Command Rank Grade
  • Beginner
     ↪ Start at this rank
     ↪ Max Playtime: 2 Hours

  • Junior
     ↪ Available from 11th July 2025, 0000hrs onwards.
     ↪ Achieve by defeating Snow Witch in Area 1
     ↪ Max Playtime: 2 Hours

  • Senior
     ↪ Available from 16th July 2025, 0000hrs onwards.
     ↪ Achieve by defeating Snow Witch in Area 2
     ↪ Max Playtime: 4 Hours

  • Veteran
     ↪ Available from 23rd July 2025, 0000hrs onwards.
     ↪ Achieve by defeating Snow Witch in Area 3
     ↪ Max Playtime: 4 Hours

  • Master and Grand Master
     ↪ Available from 30th July 2025, 0000hrs onwards.
     ↪ Achieve by defeating Snow Witch in Area 4
     ↪ Max Playtime: 8 Hours


    Reward Box Grade
    Daily Rewards from Abyssal Expedition Journal
      ↪ Expedition Supplies [Basic]
      ↪ Expedition Supplies [Intermediate]
      ↪ Expedition Supplies [Advanced]
      ↪ Expedition Supplies [Superior]
      ↪ Expedition Supplies [Special]


    Mercenary Class
    Obtain new mercenaries from NPC Norman daily.
  • Explorer Warrior
  • Explorer Magician
  • Explorer Bowman
  • Explorer Thief
  • Explorer Pirate

    Mercenary Class Grade
    The higher the grade, the higher the Fame cost. Obtain Fame from Expedition Supplies box.
  • Basic: 300
  • Intermediate: 800
  • Advanced: 1500
  • Superior: 2500
  • Special: 5000
  • Mercenary Note
    •   ↪ When you talk to NPC Norman, mercenaries matching the current Command rank will appear randomly, and you can choose to recruit one of them.
      ↪ The potential team members are selected randomly based on the members you can recruit with your current command rank.
      ↪ If it becomes the next day and you have not recruited anyone, when you talk to NPC Norman new recruit targets will be randomly selected.
      ↪ You can recruit a max of 10 members (2 each of Warrior, Mage, Bowman, Thief, Pirate according to mercenaries Rank) according to the member's rank.
      ↪ After recruiting 10 members of the same rank, that rank will no longer be displayed as a potential recruit target.

  • Additional Notice
    •   ↪ The exploration time duration reset daily at 0000hrs.
      ↪ Character rewards are ONCE per world.



    [Dawnstar Part Feast]
    Dawnstar Fountain




    30th July 2025, (After Maintenance) ~ 19th August 2025, 2359hrs

    Available to Level 101+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest.

    Once per Maple ID


  • Eliminate 1,000 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) daily to receive Memorial Coins.
  • If you accept the quest in Challengers World, additional Challengers Coins can be obtained.
  • Obtain bonus Memorial Coins: 2x the amount on the 5th and 10th Stamp, and 4x the amount on the 15th Stamp.
  • You can also use 3,000 Maple Points to get a Check-In attendance by clicking USE if you have missed a day.



    Broomy's Thrilling Great Cleanup


    9th July 2025, (After Maintenance) ~ 12th August 2025, 2359hrs



    Available to Level 101+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest.



  • Look for NPC Broomy in the event map or Event List to get the Exciting Cleaning Time event skill.
  • Eliminate 200 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) to trigger the skill up to 30 times a day.
  • Every trigger gives a set amount of EXP depending on your character level.
  • On the 30th time triggering the skill, 'Old Dolls', 'Gemstones', and 'Ancient Relics' may appear at a set chance, granting EXP Based on the outcome.



    Broomy's Thrilling Last Cleanup


    13th August 2025, 0000hrs ~ 19th August 2025, 2359hrs



    Available to Level 101+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest.



  • Look for NPC Broomy in the event map or Event List to get the Happy Cleaning Time event skill.
  • Eliminate 250 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) to trigger the skill up to 30 times a day.
  • Every trigger gives a set amount of exp depending on your character level.
  • On the 10th, 20th and 30th time triggering the skill, 'Old Dolls', 'Gemstones', and 'Ancient Relics' may appear at a set chance, granting EXP Based on the outcome.

    Champion Burning - Double Up


    30th July 2025 (After Maintenance) ~ 30th September 2025, 2359hrs



    Available to Level 101+, Zero character who has completed Chapter 2 for Story Quest


    ❗What is Champion Double Up?
    🔹 You can assign up to 3 characters in the selected World and the Challengers World where you created the character.
    🔹 You can designate one of them as the leader first.
    🔹 You can designate the remaining two as followers.

    Double Up Attendance
    🔹 Double Up Attendance check-in can only be done by the leader by hunting monsters within the level range.
    🔹 Each Champion will receive 2,500 Double Up Coins for each completed attendance. A dedicated Coin Shop is available for each Champion character.
     (7,500 total for each attendance)

    Double Up EXP Points Accumulation
    🔹 Double Up EXP Points can only be accumulated by the Leader.
    🔹 Every time the leader hunts a monster within the level range, the followers' Double Up EXP Points will increase. (Up to 100,000 per week)
    🔹 Log in as a follower to spend Double Up EXP Points and EXP.

    Exclusive Leader Benefits (Champion Double Up Leader)
    🔹 Leader will have a special skill located in the beginner tab to summon both Follower.


    🔹 Skill ends after hunting 100,000 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level).
      ↪ EXP Obtained +15%
      ↪ Damage on Normal Monsters +15%



    Note
    🔹 You can do this in the selected World and the Challengers World where you created the character!
    🔹 The designated leader and followers can never be changed to another character.
    🔹 You can only change your leader once a week from among your designated followers.
    🔹 Once understood, select I understand now. Go Assign a leader..

    CHAMPION DOUBLE UP


    IMPORTANT GUIDE

    Setting World
    1. Click Set in the Leader Box.


    2. World Confirmation will be shown. Click Yes to proceed.


    3. Type the (Current World)/Proceed.


    Setting Leader
    1. Click Set in the Leader Box.


    2. Choose the desired leader character and click SELECT.


    3. Click Yes if the desired character selection is final. If not, click No to change.


    4. After confirming the character, type (IGN)/Confirm.


    Setting Follower
    1. Click Set in the Follower Box.


    2. Choose the desired Follower character and click SELECT.


    3. You will be shown a confirmation if you want the selected character to be set as Follower.


    4. After confirming the character, type (IGN)/Proceed.



    IMPORTANT NOTE
     ↪ You cannot change the LEADER and FOLLOWERS after assigning them.
     ↪ You cannot set the same character as both LEADER and FOLLOWERS.
     ↪ You can only change the LEADER from either of the selected FOLLOWERS.
     ↪ Hyper Burning Characters CAN be selected.

    General Progression
  • Eliminate level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) with LEADER to gain points for both Follower.
  • Up to 100,000 monsters per week which resets after Wednesday 11:59p.m.
  • 1 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) = 1 Point.
  • Eliminate level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) with FOLLOWER will not gain any points.
  • Points obtained by both Follower can be converted into EXP points.
  • EXP Points gained will be based on the character's level.


    Double Up Coin
  • Eliminate 2,000 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) with LEADER 3 times a week to get up to 7,500 Double Up Coins.
  • Both Follower will obtain its own separate Double Up Coins along with the LEADER.
  • Up to 100,000 level range monsters (-20/+20 Level) can be eliminated by the LEADER per week which resets after Wednesday 11:59p.m.
  • Click the USE button to consume 3,000 Maple Points for DOUBLE UP PASS to catch up with the times you missed.
  • Both LEADER and the 2 FOLLOWER will obtain its own Double Up Coins from the DOUBLE UP PASS.

    [Coin Shop] Follower Double Up Coin Shop
  • Follower Double Up Coin Shop ends on 30th September 2025, 2359hrs.
  • Both LEADER and the 2 FOLLOWER has its own purchase limit that does not affect each other.
  • Item duration, purchase limit, functionality and tradability are as shown in game.


    The Burn CONTINUES!

    v.261 MapleStory x DAVE THE DIVER Patch Notes


    Help Dave and his crew find their way home in Save the Diver! Hunt sea creatures in the Blue Hole Exploration and turn your catches into culinary masterpieces at Bancho Sushi for big rewards. Unlock powerful skills with the New Mastery Nodes and put them to the test as you face off against Kazax once more in Ride or Die!

    NEW UPDATES

    New Mastery Nodes

    It's time to power up because New HEXA Mastery nodes have arrived!

    Hero

    • 3rd Mastery Node
      • HEXA Beam Blade
        • Launches blades that tear your enemies apart.
      • Rending Edge
        • Swordsmanship reached the extreme to leave a powerful sword scar.
    • 4th Mastery Node
      • HEXA Puncture
        • Pour your swordsman’s spirit into a forward-downward strike.
      • HEXA Final Attack
        • Chance to deliver an additional hit after a direct hit.
      • HEXA Cry Valhalla
        • Call upon the power of the ancients to defend you.

    Paladin

    • 3rd Mastery Node
      • HEXA Heaven’s Hammer
        • Slam a large hammer into the ground, creating an impact that deals damage to multiple enemies.
    • 4th Mastery Node
      • HEXA Final Attack
        • Chance to deliver a powerful additional hit upon landing a direct hit.
      • Rising Justice
        • Justice Remnant emerges due to the impact of Falling Justice.

    Dark Knight

    • 3rd Mastery Node
      • HEXA Final Attack
        • Chance to deliver an additional hit after a direct hit.
      • HEXA Revenge of the Evil Eye
        • Evil Eye counter attacks the enemy.
    • 4th Mastery Node
      • HEXA Evil Eye Shock
        • The Evil Eye lets out a scream that stuns and damages nearby enemies.

    Arch Mage (Fire, Poison)

    • 3rd Mastery Node
      • HEXA Ignite
        • Grants fire magic a chance to create a wall of fire at the target location. Does not include Inferno Aura.
      • HEXA Ifrit
        • Summons a fire Ifrit for a short time.
      • HEXA Inferno Aura
        • Channel fire chakras to burst into flame.
    • 4th Mastery Node
      • HEXA Creeping Toxin
        • Conjures a poison-attribute totem.
      • HEXA Meteor Shower
        • Summon countless meteorites to inflict intense fire damage.
      • HEXA Megiddo Flame
        • Fires a blue flame that burns the enemy to the very soul.

    Arch Mage (Ice, Lightning)

    • 3rd Mastery Node
      • HEXA Lightning Orb
        • Creates a large, unstable sphere of electricity to continuously zap enemies.
      • Cryo Shock
        • Inflict cold on the enemy then deal an intense shock with the power of strong lightning.
    • 4th Mastery Node
      • HEXA Thunder Sphere
        • Summon an orb of condensed lightning.
      • HEXA Elquines
        • Summons Elquines for a short time.

    Bishop

    • 3rd Mastery Node
      • HEXA Angelic Wrath
        • Calls down an avenging angel to strike the enemy, and creates a relic where it struck to continuously weaken the enemy.
      • HEXA Fountain of Vengeance
        • Summon a divine talisman of vengeance that punishes nearby enemies.
      • HEXA Bahamut
        • Temporarily summons Bahamut.
    • 4th Mastery Node
      • HEXA Genesis
        • A holy ray of light shines down from the sky, dealing tremendous holy damage.
      • HEXA Heaven's Door
        • Knocks on the door to the heavens to punish enemies and bless your party members at the same time.

    Bow Master

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Quiver Cartridge
        • Use a special arrowhead.
      • HEXA Phoenix
        • Temporarily summon a Phoenix.
      • Extra Quiver Cartridge: Expand Quiver Cartridge to load a special arrowhead.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Speed Mirage
        • Fire arrows fast enough to leave afterimages.
      • HEXA Gritty Gust
        • Tear nearby enemies apart with a gust of wind.

    Marksman

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Frostprey
        • Temporarily summons a Frostprey.
      • HEXA Bolt Burst
        • Fires arrows in all directions, striking multiple enemies nearby.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Final Attack: Chance to deliver an additional hit upon landing a direct attack skill.
      • HEXA High Speed Shot: Fires off a focused shot that pierces all enemies within range.

    Pathfinder

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Cardinal Torrent
        • An archery technique used to achieve high mobility. Release Swiftstrike Energy stored in your weapon as a short burst of speed that propels you to your destination, then swing your weapon to attack nearby enemies.
      • HEXA Glyph of Impalement
        • Call forth spears of dark energy imbued with the power of the Ancient Curse to attack nearby enemies.
      • HEXA Ancient Astra
        • Manifest arrows like those spoken of in legend to rain destruction upon your foes.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Shadow Raven
        • Calls forth a dark-elemental Raven for a period of time.
      • HEXA Combo Assault
        • Attack nearby enemies with your bow, then let loose a magical arrow to attack enemies in a wider range.
      • Manifest Curse
        • Completely control the cursed relic's power to materialize the curse.

    Night Lord

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Dark Flare
        • Release dark energy, for a certain period of time, to summon a large shuriken that attacks enemies nearby.
      • HEXA Showdown
        • Attacks up to 6 enemies with a shuriken and provokes them, making them untouchable.
      • Darkness Shuriken
        • A throwing star with a will appears from the darkness.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Sudden Raid
        • Call in a horde of friends to attack enemies.
      • HEXA Death Star
        • Summons 4 shurikens that combine into one giant shuriken.

    Shadower

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Dark Flare
        • Release dark energy for a certain period of time to summon a large dagger, which attacks enemies nearby.
      • HEXA Cruel Stab
        • Inflicts a brutal stab with the dagger.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Sudden Raid
        • Call in a horde of friends to attack enemies.
      • HEXA Shadow Veil
        • Summons a dark ally to deal damage over time.
      • Covert Edge
        • Deal a covert blow from the shadows.

    Dual Blade

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Blade Clone
        • Summons a dagger from the Secret Garden to deal powerful bonus damage with all your attacks.
      • Mortality
        • Yaksha, the god of the netherworld, descends to annihilate all nearby enemies.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Blade Fury
        • The secret technique of Secret Garden's tornado. Spin furiously with the two blades in your hands to damage nearby enemies.
      • HEXA Sudden Raid
        • Call in a horde of friends to attack enemies.

    Buccaneer

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Serpent Scale
        • Harnessing the power of the Sea Serpent periodically creates Serpent Scales which can be consumed to activate more powerful Sea Serpent skills.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Hook Bomber
        • Throws a punch that attacks the enemy in front with a powerful explosive energy.

    Corsair

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Brain Scrambler
        • Shoots the target in its squishy bits to deal heavy damage to it.
      • HEXA Eight-Legs Easton
        • Fires a hefty barrage of bullets.
      • HEXA Firing Orders
        • Mark your location for a Broadside bombardment.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Siege Bomber
        • Set up a stationary cannon to temporarily bombard nearby enemies.
      • HEXA Scurvy Summons
        • Summon a brave crewman from the Nautilus.
      • HEXA Nautilus Strike
        • Order the Nautilus to attack multiple enemies at once.
      • HEXA Ugly Bomb
        • Fires a really weird-looking bomb that you... where did you buy this thing?

    Cannoneer

    • 3rd Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Rolling Rainbow
        • Orders the Cannoneer's reliable assistants to summon multiple cannons and mercilessly roast enemies ahead of you.
    • 4th Job Mastery Node
      • HEXA Monkey Fury

    Skill Improvements and Changes

    • Kanna
      • HEXA Shikigami Haunting
        • Changed the amount needed to activate Shikigami Doppelganger on the 3rd hit from 5 to 20.
        • Removed the animation delay after the 3rd hit.
      • Mana Warp
        • Added Speed +22 and Speed Limit +20 at Lv.15.
        • Changed where the skill can be cancelled.
      • Circle of Suppression
        • Changed where mana is no longer consumed when activated.
      • Blossom Barrier
        • Increased the skill duration from 20 seconds to 30 seconds.
        • Increased the cooldown from 100 seconds to 120 seconds.
      • Sengoku Force, Assemble!
        • Changed to now grant fixed buffs: Critical Damage and Attack, instead of random buffs.
    • Hayato
      • Hitokiri Strike - Persist
        • Increased the buff duration from 20 seconds to 60 seconds.
      • Sengoku Force, Assemble!
        • Changed to now grant fixed buffs: Critical Damage and Attack, instead of random buffs.
    • Mo Xuan
      • Qi Projection
        • Increased the attack count per hit from 3 to 4.
        • Decreased the damage per hit at Lv. 20 from 400% to 300%.
      • Soul Art: The Conquered Self
        • Changed where the skill now temporarily enhances Qi Projection to enter The Conquered Self.
        • Increased Qi Projection damage at Lv. 30 by 55%.
        • Decreased the max number of afterimages created from 9 to 8.
      • Divine Art: Howling Storm
        • Increased the number of attacks per hit while holding the skill from 3 to 5.
        • Decreased the maximum hold duration from 5 seconds to 3 seconds.
      • HEXA Divine Art: Howling Storm
        • Improved the charge effect.
        • Increased the number of attacks per hit while the skill is pressed from 4 to 6.
        • Decreased the maximum hold duration from 3 seconds to 2 seconds.
      • Divine Arts - Enhance
        • Increased the Reincarnation’s final damage increase effect from 5% to 20%.
      • Divine Fist Disciples
        • The skill is now usable while in the air.
      • The Holy Mountain/Heir of the Divine
        • Improved the effects of Form Link and Reincarnation.
        • Added a notification popup for Form Link and Reincarnation.
    • Lynn
      • [Focus] Awaken
        • Changed where the skill can now be used on the caster.
        • Added a [Resonant] effect that increases Final Damage by approximately 30% when cast on a Focal Target, instead of the caster.
        • Increased the maximum Final Damage at Lv. 30 from 50% to 60%.
        • Changed where the Final Damage buff now applies to both the current Focal Target and yourself.
          • Increased the Final Damage buff at Lv. 30 from 5% to 10%.
        • Changed where the Final Damage increase is reduced by 50% if there is one or fewer party members, including the caster.
      • [Focus] Awaken Boost
        • Increased the Final Damage for the Focal Target from 10% to 15%.
        • Added an effect that changes in the Final Damage increase effect from a [Resonant] effect to 15%.
      • [Focus] Heal
        • Added a [Resonant] effect that recovers HP over time based on Max HP when activating the skill on the [Focal Target] instead of the caster.
      • [Focus] Forest Protection
        • Added a [Resonant] effect that grants a barrier that reduces damage taken when activating the skill on the [Focal Target] instead of the caster.
      • Beast's Rage
        • Increased the Damage at Lv. 30 from 960% to 1920%.
      • Beak Strike
        • Changed Beak Strike to temporarily enhance Peck.
          • Increases damage by 115%, greatly reduces attack intervals, and changes the attack to an area effect during the skill duration at Lv. 30.
        • Increased the number of attacks from 6 to 7.
        • Decreased the skill duration from 40 seconds to 20 seconds.
      • Predator’s Blow
        • Decreased the skill duration from 40 seconds to 30 seconds.

    Sol Erda Conversion Update

    • Changed the item name ‘HEXA Booster’ to ‘SHINE Booster’ when accessing Sol Erda Conversion via the Erda Link UI.

    • Convert your owned Sol Erda into Faint Sol Erda Energy or SHINE Boosters.
      • Only Sia Astelle characters who have completed the 6th Job Advancement can convert Sol Erda into a SHINE Booster.
    Sol Erda Converted Item Created Quantity
    1 Faint Sol Erda Energy: Tradable within world, expires the day after conversion at 12:00 AM UTC. 30
    NEW SHINE Booster: Tradable within world, expires the day after conversion at 12:00 AM UTC. 1
    • Use a SHINE Booster to summon monsters that give a large amount of EXP when defeated within 100 seconds.
      • Must be used in a map where monsters are within your level range (20 levels below and 20 levels above).
    • SHINE Boosters and HEXA Boosters are tradable within world and can be used by characters who have completed the 6th Job Advancement.
      • For example: Sia Astelle can use HEXA Boosters and Hoyoung can use SHINE Boosters.

    DAVE THE DIVER EVENTS

    Save the Diver!

    July 16 (after maintenance) - August 26 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters (Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2).

    Dave and his crew have unexpectedly washed up in Maple World... and are most definitely stranded! Grab your floaties, slap on some sunscreen, and help them find their way home!

    Quick Overview

    • The event is made up of story chapters with mission objectives that can be completed by participating in two main activities:
      • Blue Hole Exploration: Dive into the ocean to hunt fish and collect their fillets.
      • Bancho Sushi: Use the fish fillets you collected to run a sushi restaurant.
    • Completing chapters will unlock new features, story content, and exclusive event rewards!

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Save the Diver!’ from the Event List and click ‘Participate’ to start the Save the Diver! event.
      • Alternatively, accept the ‘[Save the Diver] Rescue Request’ quest by talking to Dave in any of the Major Towns (Henesys, Nameless Town, Cernium Square).
    • Upon accepting the quest, you will teleport to the event map where Dave and his party are waiting for you on their boat!
    • Feeling seasick? Talk to Cobra at any time to return to your previous location.
    • Note: Items obtained from this event expires on a fixed date instead of a set duration.

    Smartphone

    • The Smartphone will act as the main event UI. While at the event map, click the icon on the left side of the screen or press the ESC key to open the Smartphone UI.

    • The two event currencies, Gold and Diver Tokens, are displayed at the top of the screen.
      • Gold: Obtainable by participating in the Blue Hole Exploration and Bancho Sushi.
      • Diver Token: Obtainable by completing chapters.
    • The center of the Smartphone UI displays your current chapter and mission objective.
    • Use the ‘WASD’ keys to navigate through the apps and Spacebar to select an app. You can also click on the app icons directly. Available apps:
      • iDiver: Upgrade diving gear for Blue Hole Exploration.

      • Weapon Shop: Upgrade weapons for Blue Hole Exploration.

      • Codex: View all the sea creatures you’ve caught.

      • Token Shop: Spend Diver Tokens for exclusive event rewards!

    Chapters and Progression

    • There are 10 chapters, followed by an Epilogue that unlocks once all chapters are complete.
    • Chapters must be completed in order and you’ll need to complete each mission objective to move forward.
    • When a mission is complete, a checkmark will appear on your Smartphone indicating the chapter cutscene is ready.
      • Press ‘E’ or click ‘Start Story’ to watch the cutscene and claim your reward before continuing onto the next chapter.
    • Complete chapters to earn rewards and unlock features in the Blue Hole Exploration and Bancho Sushi.

    HIDDEN MISSION ALERT! Feels like something’s hiding in plain sight... Maybe it’s just waiting for a nudge?

    Back to Top

    Blue Hole Exploration

    July 16 (after maintenance) - August 26 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who have completed the ‘[Save the Diver] Rescue Request’ quest (Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2).

    They say there’s plenty of fish in the sea... so let’s swim around and find out! Dive into the Blue Hole to hunt fish, collect fillets, and discover what the deep sea has to offer.

    How to Participate

    • Defeat 1,000 monsters within your level range (20 levels below and 20 levels above) then talk to Dave at the event map and select ‘Ready to Dive’ to complete an Exploration Preparation.
      • Monster defeats only count when in a solo party or not in a party at all.
      • Exploration Preparation can be completed once a day per account.
        • Progress is shared between all characters per account.
    • To start a Blue Hole Exploration, approach the ladder on the right side of the boat and hold Spacebar.
      • All buffs are removed upon entering the Blue Hole Exploration map.
      • Fish fillets collected in the Tutorial Mode will not be kept.

    Blue Hole Exploration Minigame

    • The goal is to hunt fish, collect fillets, and return to the surface safely before oxygen or time runs out! You’ll have 60 minutes for each dive.
    • A Blue Hole Exploration can end in either success or failure, depending on how you finish the dive:
      • A dive is successful when:
        • Swim back up to the surface
        • Use an Escape Pod
        • Use the Emergency Pager
      • A dive fails when:
        • Your oxygen runs out
        • The 60-minute time limit runs out
        • You choose “Return to Boat” after giving up
    • If the dive fails, you’ll lose everything you collected during that attempt.
      • You can retry up to two times per day, so be careful out there!
    • Finish a dive successfully to receive Gold and all the fillets you collected to serve up dishes at the Bancho Sushi!

    Exploration Controls

    Function Controls and Details
    Basic Movement
    • W: Move Up
    • A: Move Left
    • S: Move Down
    • D: Move Right
    Swim Faster
    • Use W/A/S/D to move while holding Shift.
    • Swimming faster consumes additional oxygen.
    Melee / Use Knife
    • Left Mouse Button (LMB)
    • All fish can be damaged by melee attacks.
    Fire Weapon
    • Hold Right Mouse Button (RMB) to aim.
    • Press LMB to fire.
    • While holding RMB to aim, game speed will slow to help you aim.
    • Works with the equipped Harpoon, Underwater Rifle, and Red Sniper weapons.
    Switch Weapon
    • Press Tab to switch between Harpoon, Underwater Rifle, and Red Sniper weapons.
    Use Exploration Equipment
    • Press C to use the equipped Exploration Equipment item.
    Switch Exploration Equipment
    • Press R to switch between available Exploration Equipment.
    Open Diving Inventory
    • Press Tilde (~) to open up the Fish PDA and review the fish you've hunted and the meat you've obtained.
    Open Fish PDA
    • Press Esc to open up your inventory, allowing you to view your equipment and acquired fish.
    • The dive is paused while this menu is open, however time in the menu will still count against the 1-hour time limit.
    Use/Interact
    • Press Space to interact with equipment and objects found in the Blue Hole.
    • Use while at the surface to return to the boat.

    Hunting Fish and Collecting Fillets

    • Primary weapons are used to hunt fish and can be permanently upgraded with Gold through the Weapon Shop app on the Smartphone.
    Primary Weapon Type Description
    Melee Weapon

    		Basic close-range attack used for striking nearby fish
    Harpoon

    		Reel in a fish
    Rifle

    		Ranged weapon that deals damage
    • The swim speed will decrease when aiming with a Harpoon or Rifle.

    • During a dive, additional weapons and equipment can be found throughout the Blue Hole to support your exploration! These are divided into the following categories:
      • Weapon Box: Contains primary weapons for taking down tougher fish.

      • Equipment Box: Contains secondary equipment that enhance movement, damage, and survivability during an exploration.

      • General Items: Support equipment that’s ready to use.
    Weapon Box Item Description
    Kenta’s Harpoon
    • Replaces default melee weapon ‘Underwater Knife’ when equipped.
    • Deals 17 damage
    • Increases the gauge fill rate during the Harpoon pulling minigame.
    • Cannot be upgraded
    Frozen Tuna
    • Replaces default melee weapon ‘Underwater Knife’ when equipped.
    • Deals 17 damage
    • Cannot be upgraded
    Red Sniper Rifle

    • Replaces default rifle ‘Underwater Rifle’ when equipped.
    • Can be upgraded
    Equipment Box Item Description
    Oxygen Capsules

    		Restore 50% oxygen
    Underwater Scooter

    		Temporarily boosts swim speed
    Rifle Enhancement Kit

    		Temporarily increases firearm damage
    Emergency Pager

    		Call for an Escape Pod to immediately complete an exploration
    General Item Description
    Ammo Box

    		Replenish ammunition for all weapons
    Air Tank

    		Restore 100% oxygen
    Escape Pod

    		Immediately complete an exploration

    Note: All weapons and equipment obtained in a dive are temporary and only usable during the current dive.

    • There are two ways to collect fish fillets:
      • Small Fish: Automatically drop fillets when defeated.
      • Large Fish: When a fish is defeated, swim up to its carcass and collect the fillets by holding Spacebar.

    • Use a Harpoon to reel in certain fish and collect fillets through a minigame.
      • When a Harpoon hits a small fish and its remaining HP is between 1x and 2x the Harpoon’s damage, it enters “Pulling” status and a minigame is triggered.
      • Press Spacebar repeatedly to fill the gauge.
        • Success: The fish is caught and fillets are automatically collected.
        • Fail: The fish escapes and only takes 1 damage.

      • The exploration time temporarily pauses during the minigame.
      • If another fish hits you before the minigame starts, the Harpoon automatically retracts and the attempt fails.
      • Harpoons do not pierce certain enemies like jellyfish and sharks. Instead they’ll bounce off and only deal damage.
        • Exception: The Cookiecutter Shark can enter “Pulling” status.
      • Want to see what you’ve caught during your dive? Press ~ to open the Fish PDA and view all fish caught and fillets collected so far.
        • The exploration time temporarily pauses when this is open.

    Exploration Systems

    There are several factors that impact the overall results of an exploration to keep in mind. These include oxygen, depth limit, weight, and movement speed, which can all be upgraded through the iDiver app on the Smartphone.

    • Oxygen
      • The Oxygen Gauge is located at the bottom left of the screen.
      • Oxygen continuously decreases during a dive, however, it depletes faster when you:
        • Hold ‘Shift’ to swim faster
        • Take damage from fish attacks
      • Upgrade the Air Tank to increase the maximum starting oxygen.

    • Depth Limit
      • You can only explore to a specific depth based on the Diving Suit level.
      • Stronger fish live in deeper areas and have better rewards when defeated.
      • Upgrade the Diving Suit to increase the maximum depth limit that can be explored.
    • Weight (Inventory)
      • Collected ingredients add weight (kg) to the diver’s inventory
      • Your movement speed decreases when you reach or exceed the maximum weight limit.
        • A weight icon will appear above your head.
      • Items can be discarded manually in the inventory.
      • Upgrade the Waterproof Box to increase the maximum weight.

    • Movement Speed
      • Swim speed is determined by the level of the diver’s fins.
      • Upgrade fins to increase the maximum movement speed.

    Blue Hole Exploration Additional Entries

    • After completing the first Blue Hole Exploration of the day, one additional dive will be unlocked and can be completed by using one of the following:
      • Blue Hole Exploration Entry Ticket
      • Additional Ready to Dive ticket that can be purchased for 1,000 Maple Points.
    • Additional entries accumulate daily throughout the event period.

    Blue Hole Codex

    July 16 (after maintenance) - August 26 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who have completed the ‘[Save the Diver] Rescue Request’ quest (Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2).

    Got a memory like a goldfish and wondering what you’ve caught so far? Check out the Blue Hole Codex to track all your discoveries!

    How to Participate

    • Fish defeated during a Blue Hole Exploration are automatically registered to the Blue Hole Codex when the dive ends by returning to the boat.
      • Sea creatures only register if the dive ends successfully by returning to the boat.
      • Codex progress is shared between all characters within the account.
      • Fish obtained in the Tutorial Mode will not be registered to the Codex.
    • Open the Smartphone and select the Codex app to access the Blue Hole Codex.
    • Hover over a creature’s icon to see where they will appear.
    • Click on a creature's image to view:
      • How many times it has been caught
      • Ecological information

    Blue Hole Codex Rewards

    • Complete an entire row of creatures to earn a Row Completion Reward.
    • Register all creatures to earn the Full Completion Reward!
    • Reward claim records are shared between all characters within the account.

    Bancho Sushi

    July 16 (after maintenance) - August 26 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who have completed the ‘[Save the Diver] Rescue Request’ quest (Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2).

    Yes CHEF it’s time to cook! What’s on the menu today? Let’s hope it’s not a flop. Use the fish you’ve caught to prep dishes, serve customers, and make Bancho proud. Order up!

    How to Participate

    • Automatically enter the Bancho Sushi restaurant after completing a Blue Hole Exploration.
      • Alternatively, move to the left side of the boat in the event map and select ‘Sushi’ to enter.
    • The Bancho Sushi restaurant can only be accessed after finishing a dive.
    • You can enter the Bancho Sushi restaurant again if you haven’t opened for business (started taking customers), but once you open, you must complete the business day before diving again at the Blue Hole.

    Bancho Sushi Minigame

    The Bancho Sushi minigame is divided into three phases:

    1. Kitchen Preparation: Set your menu, upgrade dishes, and hire staff.
    2. Running the Restaurant: Serve dishes, clean up messes, pour green tea, and refill wasabi.
    3. Closing Time and Payout: View your earnings and performance.

    1. Kitchen Preparation

    Controls Function
    Spacebar Select
    C Cancel
    ESC Smartphone/Cancel
    Left Ctrl Enhance Dish/Hire Staff
    1 Menu
    2 Hire Staff

    Menu Settings

    • Press 1 to open the Menu UI
    • You’ll start with 5 menu slots unlocked and can unlock up to 7 as you progress through the chapters.
    • Add dishes in a menu slot using fish fillets collected from a Blue Hole Exploration.
    • The Basic Menu items Norimaki and Green Tea are located to the right. They do not count towards the Menu Slot limit.
    • Removing a dish from the Menu does not consume ingredients.

    Dish Enhancements

    • Select a dish and press Ctrl or click Enhance Dish to increase the price of your dish.
    • Dishes can be enhanced up to Lv. 5 and will require more fillets at higher levels.
      • Norimaki and Green Tea are fixed at Lv. 1 and cannot be enhanced.
      • Pianus Carpaccio and Steamed Pianus Head are always Lv. 5 and cannot be enhanced.

    Hosting Parties

    • On specific dates, you can host special Parties where certain dishes will sell at a boosted price! There are 3 types of parties, each focusing on a specific fish:
      • Day 15: Jellyfish Party
        • Dishes sell for 5x the normal price.
        • Applies to sushi made from Fried Egg Jellyfish, White Spotted Jellyfish, and Comb Jelly.
      • Day 20: Tuna Party
        • Dishes sell for 2.5x the normal price.
        • Applies to sushi made from Yellowfin Tuna and Bluefin Tuna.
      • Day 25: Shark Party
        • Dishes sell for 1.5x the normal price.
        • Applies to sushi made from Whitetip Reefshark, Smooth Hammerhead, Copper Shark, Thresher Shark, Longnose Sawshark, Zebra Shark, Cookiecutter Shark, Frilled Shark, Rhinochimaeridae, and Megamouth Shark.
      • Parties repeat every 15 in-story days (ie: Day 30 will be a Jellyfish Party, Day 35 will be a Tuna Party, Day 40 will be a Shark party...).
    • A banner will appear at the top right corner of your screen 3 days before a party begins and what type of party is coming!

    Hiring and Placing Staff

    • Press 2 or use the Hire Staff button to view the employee list.
    • Staff can be hired using Gold and any hired staff will be placed in the waiting room.
    • Place your staff members in either the Hall or Kitchen employee slot using Spacebar.
      • Up to 2 employees can be placed at each location.
    • Additional staff slots will unlock as you progress through the chapters.

    2. Running the Restaurant

    Controls Function
    W Hold to grate Wasabi
    S Hold to pour Green Tea
    A Move to the left
    D Move to the right
    Left Shift Hold while pressing A or D to move faster
    E Hold to start business
    A + D Repeatedly press both keys at the same time to clean up a mess
    Q Hold to discard food
    Spacebar Select/Talk
    C Cancel
    ESC

    Starting Business

    • Press E to open the Bancho Sushi for service!
    • A warning will pop up if the menu isn’t fully set.
    • The first playthrough will start in Tutorial Mode.

    Pouring Green Tea

    • Some customers request for Green Tea before ordering food.
    • Press Spacebar near the customer then hold S to start the pouring minigame.
    • The tip amount you receive is dependent on how close you fill to the green zone.
    • If the Complaint Gauge fills, you will fail the pouring minigame and the customer won’t accept the Green Tea.

    Serving Dishes

    • Orders are cooked automatically by Bancho and the kitchen staff. There are two gauges indicating:
      • A dish is currently being made
      • A dish is ready

    • When dishes are ready, walk to the Kitchen area and press Spacebar to pick it up. Then walk up to the customer with the correct order and press Spacebar to serve it.
    • Delays will increase the Complaint Gauge! If the gauge is completely filled, the customer leaves with no tip, so we gotta go fast!
    • Throw away any dish by pressing Q.

    Cleaning Messes

    • Some customers leave messy tables which delay new customers from sitting!
    • Press Spacebar at any dirty table, then repeatedly press A + D to clean.
    • Receive Gold by cleaning up messes!

    Wasabi Refill

    • Wasabi is used for every dish and will need to be refilled consistently. Keep an eye on the Wasabi Gauge to the right to make sure it doesn’t run out.
      • If the Wasabi Gauge runs out, the kitchen staff stops cooking.
    • Press Spacebar at the Wasabi station to trigger a minigame. Repeatedly press W to refill the Wasabi!

    3. Closing Time and Payout

    • Bancho Sushi ends when all customers have been served and leave or the 2-minute timer runs out.
    • A results summary will appear at the end of the session, showing your restaurant's performance, revenue for the day, and how much Gold was earned!
    • After completing Story Chapter 10, you’ll also earn Diver Tokens equal to the Gold earned as an additional reward.

    Back to Top

    RIDE OR DIE EVENTS

    Ride or Die

    July 16 (after maintenance) - August 26 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 200 and above (Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2).

    Kazax has returned with new powers and an even greater threat! A new ally, Inspector Libae, has a plan to stop him. Harness the power of the Mapae and fight back to protect Maple World!

    Quick Overview

    • Take on up to 5 bosses each week by choosing your difficulty level and setting challenges.
    • The higher the difficulty and number of challenges, the greater the rewards will be and a higher final score you'll receive!
    • Earn rewards like Inspector Coins, Kazax’s Energy Fragments, and weekly Inspector Supply Boxes based on your final score.

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Ride or Die’ from the Event List and click ‘Participate’ to start the Ride or Die event.
    • Upon accepting the quest, you’ll be teleported to the event map, where you’ll meet Libae, a new inspector who urgently needs your help to save Maple World!

    Setting Boss Difficulty and Challenges

    • Face off against up to 5 bosses per week by choosing your difficulty and how many challenges you want to take on. The 5 bosses you can challenge are:
      • Papulatus
      • Vellum
      • Horntail
      • Darknell
      • Magnus
    • There are four difficulties to choose from:
      • Code B: Easy
      • Code A: Normal
      • Code S: Hard
      • Code X: Extreme
        • Code X Requirements: Only your weapon, secondary weapon, and emblem can be equipped for this challenge. Swapping equipment will be disabled during battle.
        • Test your strength and limits in Code X to earn the highest reward box and a large number of Kazax fragments! With different bosses and fewer challenges this time, Code X is the perfect chance to push for a high score.

    • Ready for a challenge? You can set up to 15 challenges and one will be randomly assigned to you during each run. The following challenges are available:

    • The score multiplier for challenges have been increased, so the more challenges you take on, the higher your weekly score will be!
    • You have a total of 20 lives shared across all 5 bosses per week. If you lose them all, you’re done for the week!
      • Use Practice Mode to familiarize yourself with the bosses! Speak with Libae to adjust the difficulty level and challenges as needed.
        • Practice Mode is unavailable for Code X difficulty.
    • An Investigation Result summary will appear when you successfully defeat a boss, showing your current Investigation Score and Weekly Score. Scores are calculated based on:
      • Chosen difficulty
      • Number of challenges set
      • Death count

    Althea's Support

    • Althea is here to support you during fights! Once inside the boss map, you’ll receive Althea’s Support, a special skill that charges support up to Lv. 3 as you fight.
      • Charge the skill by collecting support! The more support you receive, the more powerful Althea’s Support skill effect will be!

    • The amount of support required to charge each level is 150.
      • For every 15 support gained, one skill gauge slot fills.
      • Receive a small amount of support at regular intervals.
      • Receive a great amount of support when your character touches a summoned object.
        • The object spawns at a random location every 30 seconds and disappears after a certain amount of time.

    • Once the gauge is full, press the Interact key to activate one of Althea’s support skills at random. These help clear summoned enemies and disrupt Kazax’s interference.
    • Right-click the skill icon to toggle between automatic or manual activation.

    Kazax's Interference

    • Kaxaz isn’t going to fight fair, so stay sharp! He’ll appear alongside bosses and randomly uses skills that interfere with your fight.

    Weekly Total Score Rewards

    • Defeat bosses to also earn usable items and Silver, Bronze, or Gold Inspector Coins which can be spent at the Coin Shop for exclusive rewards!
    • Each week after the event reset, you'll receive a Weekly Total Score which will determine:
      • Which Inspector's Supply Box you receive
      • How many Kazax's Energy Fragments you earn

    • There are six levels of Inspector’s Supply Boxes that can be obtained. Score higher to receive higher-level boxes.
      • You can only claim 1 box a week per account. Rewards can only be claimed after the event weekly reset.
        • Rewards for Week 6 can be claimed immediately after completing that week's challenge.
      • [Updated 7/22/25] Note: The final score and participation count for Week 1 will be calculated from July 16 (after maintenance) - July 22 at 11:59 PM UTC.

    MORNING STAR BANQUET EVENTS

    Morning Star Banquet

    June 11 - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who completed ‘Gob’s Call’ quest or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    Are y’all HUNGRY? Our Morning Star Feast has begun and it's time to pig out! Join us on our daily feast and claim some delicious rewards~

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Morning Star Feast’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to begin.
      • Alternatively, you can talk to the Head Servant NPC located in the Event Map, Imperial Villa: Hanging Gardens, and complete the ‘[Morning Star] Perfect Feast Prep’ quest.
    • Keep up with your progress by clicking ‘Morning Star Feast’ from the Event List.
    • All characters within your account share your progress!
    • Note: Items obtained from this event expires on a fixed date instead of a set duration.

    Morning Star Feast

    • Daily Feast Prep
      • You can complete your Daily Feast Prep by clicking ‘Daily Feast Prep’ from the Event UI from the respective day. Upon checking in your Daily Feast Prep, you will receive the following:
        • 3x EXP Coupon (30 min) (x3)
        • Morning Light skill points (x5)
        • Starlight skill points (x5)
      • The Daily Feast Prep can be completed 5 times a week per account. You can obtain set rewards based on your cumulative Daily Feast Prep count.
      • You can claim these rewards by clicking the ‘Claim’ button, then select between the Memento Coin and the Daily Feast Prep reward item.
        • Please keep in mind, you will not be able to change your claimed item after selecting!
      • The Memento Coin quantity will differ from each Daily Feast Prep depending on the reward item.
      • Daily Feast Prep can be done up to 50 times overall within the event period.
    • Special Feast Prep
      • Defeat 2,000 monsters within your level range (20 levels below and 20 levels above) to complete a check-in. Upon checking in your Special Feast Prep, you will receive the following:
        • Memento Coin x1,000
      • Memento Coins can be used to exchange for various items within the Memento Coin Exchange shop!
      • Each check-in can be completed up to 3 times a week per account and cleared 3 times at once. Special Feast Prep can be done up to 30 times overall within the event period.
      • Complete all of the Special Feast Prep and you can obtain Hyper Burninator x1
        • Burning perks will be available until November 11, 2025.
    Special Feast Prep Check-in records reset every Wednesday at 12:00 AM UTC
    • Daily Feast Pass and Special Feast Pass
      • Missed a day of the Daily or Special Feast Prep? Use 3,000 Maple Points to purchase either the Daily Feast Prep or the Special Feast Prep check-in!
      • The total number of missed check-ins and Daily/Special Feast Passes available for purchase reset every Wednesday at 12:00 AM UTC each week.

    Daily Feast Prep Rewards

    • You can claim these items anytime within the event period.
    • You can choose to claim either the daily feast prep reward item or the memento coin.

    Morning Star Fountain

    July 16 (after maintenance) - August 5 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who participated in ‘Morning Star Feast’ quest or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    The Morning Star Fountain is pilin' up with these Memento Coins and it's time to clear them out! We can keep the fountain clean, gather these coins and exchange them for even more rewards!

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Morning Star Fountain’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to begin.
      • Alternatively, you can talk to the Head Servant NPC located in the Event Hub Map, Imperial Villa: Hanging Gardens.
    • Defeat 1,000 enemies near your level (20 levels above and 20 levels below), to clean up and obtain the Memento Coins!
      • Check-ins can be completed once a day per account and cleared 15 times overall within the event period.
      • Your check-ins and reward claim records are shared with all characters within the account.
    • Too busy cleaning up your actual room? No worries! Use 3,000 Maple Points to purchase a Fountain Pass to complete a missed check-in.

    Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up and Breumi's Clean Up Finale

    Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up Duration: July 16 (after maintenance) - August 19 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Breumi’s Clean Up Finale Duration: August 20 at 12:00 PM UTC - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who completed ‘Morning Star Banquet’ quest or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    Help tidy up in Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up, then take it to the next level during Breumi’s Clean Up Finale because it's not done until it sparkles. More dust, more rewards, let’s get cleaning!

    How to Participate

    • You can begin the ‘Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up’ and the ‘Breumi’s Clean Up Finale’ during their respective start dates!
    • Select ‘Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up’ or ‘Breumi’s Clean Up Finale’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to begin.
    • Talk to Breumi to receive a skill that automatically activates in hunting zones:
      • During Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up, recieve the Swish Swish skill.
      • During Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up Finale, receive the (Final) Swish Swish skill.
    • Defeat 250 monsters near your level (20 levels above or below) to fill your gauge and receive an EXP reward. This can be done up to 30 times per day.
      • Upon the 30th use, you’ll receive bonus EXP!

    Rewards and Bonuses

    • During Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up:
      • Gain EXP and a chance to obtain the Ancient Artifact Reward once a day based on a set chance.
    • During Breumi’s Exciting Clean Up Finale:
      • Gives even greater EXP! On the 10th, 20th, and 30th activations, a bonus effect will be triggered that grants a large amount of EXP and randomly activates one of three fever skills:
        • Worn Dolls
        • Jewel Ore
        • Ancient Artifacts

    Morning Starlight Harvest

    June 11 - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters who participated in the ‘Morning Star Feast’ or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    Not totally full from the Daily Morning Star Feast rewards?? Let’s make room for some sweet event buffs with Morning Starlight Harvest!

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Morning Star Harvest’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to begin.
      • Alternatively, you can talk to Angelo located in Imperial Villa: Hanging Gardens and complete the ‘[Morning Starlight Harvest] Angelo’s Request’ quest.
    • Keep up with your progress by clicking ‘Morning Star Harvest’ from the Event List.
    • When you complete the Daily Feast Prep from the ‘Morning Star Feast’ event, you will receive the following:
      • Morning Light skill points (x5)
      • Starlight skill points (x5)
    • Use the Morning Light and Starlight to activate the Morning Light Phantom skill effect.
    • The activated skill effects can be enhanced by using any owned Morning Light or Starlight and leveled up skill effects provides more powerful benefits.
    • The Morning Light Phantom skill is a passive buff skill that can be used until August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC.

    Event Buffs

    How to Obtain Morning Light Phantom

      • Characters within the same world that complete the Morning Starlight Harvest quest will be granted the Morning Light Phantom skill.
      • The Morning Star Phantom skill can be viewed from the Beginner Skill window, with benefits only applied to characters that learned the skill.
      • Purchase count for both Morning Light and Starlight is reset every Thursday at 12:00 AM UTC.
      • You can purchase the amount you need with 1,000 Maple Points each, by clicking on the [Purchase Morning Light] or [Purchase Star Light] buttons from the Morning Starlight Harvest UI.
      • Purchase count accumulates throughout the event.

    Note

      • After defeating Lotus (Hard) or a higher difficulty boss, Sol Erda Energy is dropped by defeating the boss loot box.
      • The stats, Monster Collection Capture Chance Increase and Bonus coins upon completing Legion weekly missions perks, cannot be activated in Challenger World.
      • The Arcane River Daily Mission Rewards and Grandis Daily Mission Rewards skill effects are applied once a day in each world and are applied when first completing a daily mission.
        • If you decline, you can still claim the reward with another character in the same world after completing the quest or a different daily quest.
      • The Arcane River and Grandis Daily Mission Reward skills offer an EXP boost and bonus Symbol distribution. These perks can be selectively applied to different characters and daily quests when you complete them.
      • The Arcane River Daily Mission Reward skill only applies the EXP boost perk upon completing a daily quest in the Tenebris area.
      • The Grandis Daily Mission Rewards skill only applies to Cernium, Hotel Arcus, Odium, Shangri-La, Arteria, Carcion, and Tallahart area daily quests.
      • You cannot get the additional rewards for daily quests that are already completed before activating the skill effect.
      • Legion Coins that are obtained from the Bonus coins upon completing Legion weekly missions perk do not apply to Legion Coin related achievements.

    Victory Badge Exchange

    June 29 - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Shop availability: June 11 - August 27 at 2:00 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    Have ya’ll been doing your weekly bosses?! Well I hope you are because once you defeat your bosses, you can earn Victory and Special Badges to exchange for various rewards! Easy gains.

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Victory Badge Exchange’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to begin.
      • Alternatively, you can Access the Victory Badge Exchange by talking to Mallon located at the Imperial Villa: Hanging Gardens.

    How to Obtain Victory Badges

    • Defeat weekly bosses to earn Victory Badges or Special Victory Badges. The number of badges distributed depends on the hardest difficulty a boss has been defeated.
      • Weekly boss defeats only count when in a solo party or not in a party at all.
      • You can also claim Victory and Special Victory Badge when taking on a boss in practice mode.
      • Players who reach the death count limit or leave the battle before the boss is defeated won’t be eligible to receive badges.
    • After defeating a weekly boss, talk to Mallon to claim your Victory Badges.
    • Each week, you can claim up to 2,000 Victory Badges and 50 Special Victory Badges per account.
      • The badges can only be used within the world where they are obtained in.
      • Victory and Special Victory Badges can only be earned during the event period.
    • If you have already claimed Victory or Special Victory Badges this week and you defeat a boss that gives more badges, you’ll be able to only claim the difference between the two amounts.
      • Example 1: You claimed 600 badges for defeating Normal Lotus, then defeated Easy Lucid which gives 900 badges. You’ll receive 300 additional badges which is the difference between the two boss rewards.
      • Example 2: You claimed 600 badges for defeating Normal Lotus, then defeated Normal Damien. No additional badges will be granted since the Victory Badge distributed amount are the same for the two bosses.
    • Victory Badges and Special Victory Badges can be earned from the following bosses:

    BURNING EVENTS

    Burning Express

    August 13 at 12:00 AM UTC - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 101 and above characters or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    Get ready to feel the burn this summer!! The Burning Express is here, and it’s your ticket to those scorching hot rewards.

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘[Burning Express] Growth Acceleration’ from the Event List and click ‘Participate’ to start.
      • Alternatively, you can start by accepting the ‘[Burning Express] Growth Acceleration’ quest and talking to Maple Administrator via Quick Move.
    • You can check your progress by opening the Burning Express UI at any time!

    • Defeat 1,000 monsters near your level (20 levels above or 20 levels below) and click on the ‘Check-In’ button through the event UI to complete a check-in for the day.
      • Each account can check-in once a day and the record of completed check-in’s are shared between characters within the same account.
      • Monster defeats only count when in a solo party or not in a party at all.
    • Did you miss a day? No problem! Use 3,000 Maple Points to use a Burning Pass for any missed check-ins.
    • The Flame Pass can be purchased for 29,900 Maple Points to unlock additional rewards for each completed daily check-in!
    Burning Express Check-in records reset daily at 12:00 AM UTC

    Burning Express and Flame Pass Rewards

    • You can claim the burning express and flame pass rewards at any time within the event period!

    Hyper Burning MAX

    June 11 - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Characters that meet one of the below criteria.

    1. Characters who were newly created during the event period
    2. Existing Lv. 200 - 258 character (For Zero character, one must be Lv. 200 - 258 and must have completed Story Quest Act 2)
    3. Sia Astelle characters cannot participate in Hyper Burning MAX.

    How to Set Up Hyper Burning MAX Character

    • Click ‘Set as Hyper Burning MAX’ to create your Hyper Burning MAX Character.
    • Challenger World UI

    • Interactive and Heroic Worlds UI

    Hyper Burning MAX Character Perks

    • 1+4 Level-up
      • Hyper Burning MAX characters can gain 4 extra levels for each level up from Lv. 10 to 260.
        • Levels from Lv. 1-10 will only increase by 1.
      • Zero characters will level up by 1 before Lv. 200, and can receive 1+4 level up perk after Lv. 200.
    • Level-Up Support rewards are distributed to all Hyper Burning MAX characters
      • You can get all of the following rewards by clicking the START button from the Hyper Burning MAX event UI.
      • NOTE:
        • Zero characters cannot use the Frozen Weapon Box & Frozen Secondary Weapon Box within the Legendary Cryptic Chest, or the 15-Star Fafnir Weapon Box within the 15-Star Root Abyss Set Box (Time-Restricted).
        • For existing characters that already have the Eternal Flame Ring, cannot use the coupon.
    • Reach the level achievements as a Hyper Burning MAX character and obtain rewards!
      • You can get an even more enhanced level achievement reward in Challenger World.
      • When an existing character is set as Hyper Burning MAX, you cannot claim the level rewards for levels you already reached.
        • For example, when a Lv. 235 character is set as Hyper Burning MAX, you cannot claim the level rewards for Levels 200 - 235.

    Tera Blink

    June 11 - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Newly created characters Lv. 10 and above that have been registered as Hyper Burning MAX characters or new Hyper Burning MAX Zero characters created after June 11, 2025 that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    How to Participate

    • Accept the ‘[Tera Blink] World Inside the Hat’ quest from Event List UI or talk to Spiegelmann located in Henesys or Nameless Town.
    • After completing the ‘[Tera Blink] World Inside the Hat’ quest, speak to Spiegelmann to move to the map.
      • You can stay up to 40 minutes at one time in the event map.
      • You can freely enter and exit the event map by talking to NPC Spiegelmann.
    • All skill and buff effects given through the mission are collected and removed when you exit the event map.

    Tera Blink: World Inside the Hat

    • There are 23 missions within the World Inside the Hat.
    • Clearing each mission gives a large amount of EXP and some will reward items as well.
    • Note: Characters such as Cadena, Ark, and Illium will not be able to earn EXP in the World Inside the Hat if they have not completed their job tutorial quests.

    Tera Blink Rewards

    Completing Spiegelmann's Missions

    • Spiegelmann's Power Elixir x1000: Untradable, Permanent.
    • Dazzling Hat (Pet): Untradable, Permanent, 90-day magic duration.
    • Dazzling Hat's Aura (Pet Equipment): Untradable, Permanent.
    • Spiegelmann's Hat Chair: Tradable within world, Permanent.
    • Spiegelmann's Dazzling Hat Effect: Untradable, Permanent.

    Item Burning

    June 11 - November 11 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 200 and above characters that completed ‘A Greater Power’ or Zero characters that completed Story Quest Act 2.

    Make sure your equipment is just as strong as you are with Item Burning!

    How to Participate

    • Select ‘Get your Item Burning Box’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to begin.
    • Receive up to 8 kinds of Challenger Equipment for your character when you use the Item Burning Box.
      • The Item Burning Box is tradable within worlds but the equipment obtained when the box is opened is untradable.
    • After receiving your equipment, you can try the level achievement missions and boss defeat missions!
      • Your progress for these missions can be viewed from the Event List.

    Challenger Equipment

    • Eight (8) types of equipment depending on your job will be distributed.
      • Challenger Weapon
      • Hat
      • Top
      • Bottom
      • Gloves
      • Shoes
      • Cape
      • Shoulder Accessory
    • For Zero characters only, the ‘Apply’ button will appear on the Item Burning UI to apply Lapis/Lazuli Challenger Equipment Set Effect when another equipment Set Effect is applied.
      • If the Lapis/Lazuli Challenger Equipment Set Effect is already applied to the Zero character, the Lapis/Lazuli Challenger Equipment Set application button is deactivated.
      • Bonus Stats for the distributed equipment items are granted as predetermined stats that correspond with each character's Job, and restrictions apply for Item Drop, Sell, Extract, Scroll use, Star Force enhancement, Transfer Hammer, Equipment Transmission, Bonus Stats resetting, and Potential resetting.
      • The distributed Challenger Equipment have the following enhancement/potential applied.

    Challenger World

    June 11 - September 24 at 2:00 PM UTC

    Challenger World Mission: June 11 - September 23 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: New characters created in Challenger World during the event period.

    Challenger World has officially made its way to Global MapleStory! It’s now available in both Interactive AND Heroic Worlds with their usual World perks and restrictions still in effect. Think of it as Burning World but more rewards, faster growth, and now available to everyone!

    How to Participate

    • Choose to play in either Challenger-Heroic or Challenger-Interactive. Both follow the same perks, restrictions, prices, and systems as their respective world counterparts.
      • New accounts created in Challenger-Heroic will not receive the Heroic Gift Box. This reward is exclusive to Kronos and Hyperion Heroic servers.
    • Once a Challenger World is chosen, all characters created there can only be played within that same world. You cannot switch or create characters in the other Challenger World.
      • For example: If your first character was created in Challenger-Heroic, you will still not be able to access Challenger-Interactive even if all characters are deleted. So choose carefully!!!
    • Up to 5 characters can be created in Challenger World.
      • Character Slot Expansion Coupons cannot be used.
    • After the Challenger World event ends, all characters will be automatically moved to the Challenger Leap Zone and the following will be unavailable:
      • Character Growth Items
      • Cash Inventory
      • Auction House
      • Delivery Package Storage

    Challenger World Perks and Rewards

    1. All Challenger World characters receive a special Challenger Skill, which is automatically removed upon World Leap:
      • EXP obtained increased to 1.5x rate.
      • +50 ATT/Magic ATT
      • Normal Enemy Damage +30%
      • Boss Damage +30%
      • Ignore Defense +30%
      • Critical Rate +30%
      • Critical Damage +30%
      • Buff Duration +30%
      • Knockback Resistance +100%
      • All Stats +50
      • Max HP & MP +2500
    2. In the Maple Guide recommended hunting zones for Lv. 259 and below, maps are instanced for each player and up to 10 per map.
      • In Grandis maps, up to 8 players can share the same map.
    3. Upon creation, Challenger characters can claim starter gear by clicking the ‘Claim Creation Reward’ button in the event UI. Each of the 5 Challenger characters can claim the rewards once and deleting a character will not reset the reward limit. Receive the following:
      • Pearl Maple Armor Set Box: Untradable, 7-day duration.
        • Pearl Maple Hat: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Pearl Maple Suit: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Pearl Maple Cape: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Pearl Maple Gum: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Pearl Maple Pendant: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Pearl Maple Buckle: Untradable, Permanent.
      • Power Elixir x1000: Untradable, Permanent.
      • Spell Trace x1000: Tradable, Permanent.
    4. The free gains don’t stop there because you can create up to 3 Tera Burning characters to level from 10-200 and gain 2 levels per level-up! Claim Tera Burning rewards by clicking the ‘Claim Your Tera Burning Gift!’ button in the event UI to receive the following:
      • Mysterious Cryptic Chest: Untradable, 7-day duration.
        • Snail Pet: Untradable, 30-day duration.
      • Lv. 30 Equipment Box: Untradable, expires September 24 at 2:00 PM UTC.
        • Level 30 Equipment: Untradable, Permanent.
      • Legendary Cryptic Chest: Untradable, expires September 24 at 2:00 PM UTC.
        • Frozen Hat: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Frozen Cape: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Frozen Suit: Untradable, Permanent.
        • Frozen Weapon Box: Untradable, 7-day duration.
        • Frozen Secondary Weapon Box: Untradable, 7-day duration.
      • Root Abyss Set Box (Time-Restricted): Untradable, expires September 24 at 2:00 PM UTC.
        • Root Abyss Hat: Untradable, 90-day duration.
        • Root Abyss Top: Untradable, 90-day duration.
        • Root Abyss Bottom: Untradable, 90-day duration.
        • Fafnir Weapon Box (Time-Restricted): : Untradable, 7-day duration.
      • Eternal Flame Title Coupon: Untradable, expires September 24 at 2:00 PM UTC.
        • Eternal Flame: Untradable, Permanent.

    Challenger World Missions

    • Participate in multiple Challenger World Missions by selecting ‘Challenger World’ from the Event List UI and clicking ‘Participate’ to begin.
    • There are three types of Challenger World Missions available:
      • Level Mission
      • Boss Mission
      • Hunting Mission
    • Earn rewards for completing each mission as you push your limits in Challenger World.
      • Rewards can be claimed until September 23, 2025 11:59 PM UTC.

    • Level Mission
      • Reach specific level milestones with your Challenger World character for Challenger Points and Coins. Open the Challenger World UI to automatically complete the Level Mission.
    Level Reached Challenger Points Given Challenger Coins Given

      • Defeat specific bosses with your Challenger World character for Challenger Points and Coins. Open the Challenger World UI to automatically complete the Boss Mission.

    • NEW Hunting Mission - 2x Points Event
      • Defeat 1,000 enemies near your level (20 levels above and 20 levels below), then click the ‘[Mission Complete]’ button within the Challenger World UI to complete a Hunting Mission.
        • Completing Hunting Missions now rewards 2x the Challenger Points. You’ll receive 200 Challenger Points instead of 100 starting July 16 (after maintenance) - September 23 at 11:59 PM UTC.
      • The Hunting Mission can be done once a day and up to 5 times a week per account.
      • Missed a daily hunting mission? Use 3,000 Maple Points to complete a missed daily hunting mission.

    Challenger World Tier Rewards

    • The amount of Challenger Points you own determines your Tier. Earn Challenger Points from completing Challenger World Missions to increase your Tier Rank and unlock even more rewards.
    • Reaching the Emerald Tier and above allows characters in the same world outside of Challenger World to also claim the rewards.
      • For example, if playing on Challenger-Interactive, characters in Scania, Bera, Aurora, Elysium, and Solis can claim them!
    • Additional rewards can be claimed as you reach higher Challenger Tiers, but the rewards may vary depending on the world where they are claimed.
      • The Ultimate Legion Growth Potion reward displays an additional reward agreement window only in Hyperion and Kronos worlds.
      • If the rewards are claimed in Hyperion, the quantity of Ultimate Legion Growth obtained increases from 10 to 15. When accepted, the reward cannot be claimed in Challenger-Heroic or Kronos.

    Challenger World Leap

    • There will be two Challenger World Leap events for Challenger World characters:
      • 1st Challenger World Leap: August 27 (after maintenance) - September 23 at 11:59 PM UTC
      • 2nd Challenger World Leap: September 24 (after maintenance) - October 16 at 11:59 PM UTC
    • The Challenger World event will end September 23 at 11:59 PM UTC. All characters after this date, will be moved to the leap zone.

    World Leap Details

    • Only characters Lv. 130 and above and up to 5 characters can World Leap.
    • If there are no open character slots, one will be added automatically.
      • If your character slots are full, you cannot World Leap.
    • The following items will not transfer:
      • Items and Mesos in Cash Inventory, Auction House, or Delivery Package
      • Background obtained from coupons, unless extracted through the Mover NPC and transferred when leaping.
    • Characters cannot transfer if:
      • They’re in or requesting to join a guild.
      • They are the Guild Master.
    • Event coins and shared skills will carry over to the destination world.
    • Characters that are not transferred by the World Leap deadline will be deleted.
    • Characters with the following items in their inventory cannot World Leap
      • Mystical Cube
      • Karma Solid Cube
      • Karma Bonus Mystical Cube
      • Karma Star Force 17-Star Enhancement (Lv. 160)
      • Challenger Lv. 4 Special Skill Ring Selector Coupon
      • Challenger Ring of Restraint
      • Challenger Continuous Ring
      • Challenger Weapon Jump S Ring
      • Challenger Weapon Jump D Ring
      • Challenger Weapon Jump I Ring
      • Challenger Weapon Jump L Ring

    OTHER EVENTS

    Tinkerer's Chest (Interactive and Challenger-Interactive Worlds)

    August 15 6:00 PM UTC - September 11 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 33 and above characters who obtained a Tinkerer's Chest from the Marvel Machine (Available in Interactive and Challenger-Interactive Worlds).

    How to Participate

    • Accept the '[Tinker's Set] Tinker Til You Drop' quest by talking to Yulia in any of the Major Towns (Henesys, Nameless Town, Cernium Square, etc). She'll ask you to defeat 200 monsters within your level range (20 levels below and 20 levels above) and in exchange she'll reward you a random Belt or Shoulder Accessory.
    • The are 5 different colors for the gear given and the tiers are:
      • Yellow → Green → Blue → Red → Black
    • Each exchange uses 1 Tinkerer’s Chest. This quest is repeatable too!
    • All items are Lv. 100, comes with 1 unhammered upgrade slot, and are untradeable once equipped.

    Upgrading Gear

    • You can upgrade gear obtained from Yuli for even better stats!
    • Bring your current Tinkerer item and 1 extra Tinkerer’s Chest to Yulia for a chance to upgrade the item's color tier.
      • Upgrade attempts can fail or even downgrade your item.
    • Wearing a belt and shoulder accessory of the same color grants a set bonus!

    Wish Upon a Shooting Star

    June 11 - August 26 at 11:59 PM UTC

    Requirement: Lv. 20 and above Sia Astelle characters.

    The stars are aligning to guide you forward on your Maple journey. As you follow the path of the shooting stars, you’ll collect wishes that grant powerful rewards!

    How to Participate

    • As Sia Astelle, select ‘Wish Upon a Shooting Star’ from the Event List UI and click ‘Participate’ to start.
      • Alternatively, you can start by accepting the ‘[Wish Upon a Shooting Star] Lead Wish’ quest and talking to Sirius located in Oort.
    • Use the ‘Wish Upon a Shooting Star’ button in the event list to track your event progress at any time!
    • The event UI is split into two sections:
      • Wishes of Progress: Level-based progression rewards
      • Wishes of Style: Fashion and cosmetic rewards.

    Wishes of Progress

    • For Wishes of Progress, you’ll earn rewards as you reach level milestones throughout the event. There are two types of rewards available:
      • Basic Rewards
      • Premium Pass Rewards
    • The Premium Pass can be purchased for 25,000 Maple Points where you can receive additional rewards and special perks:
      • Premium Pass Rewards
      • Access to the Premium Login Event
      • Hunting Perks:
        • +50% Bonus EXP
        • +10% Increased Item Drop Rate
        • Revive in Place Upon Death
      • Note: The Premium Pass can only be purchased once per account. The additional rewards and special perks only apply to the Sia Astelle character that purchased the Premium Pass and are not shared with other characters within the account.
    • Complete specific level milestones within each constellation to unlock additional rewards. There are three constellations to complete:
      • Alchiba
      • Formalhaut
      • Sadalmelik
    Level Basic Reward Quantity Premium Pass Reward Quantity
